21/05/2024, 09:46 - Saksham Singh Tomar Clg: #include <iostream>
using namespace std;

int main() {
    float marks[5], total = 0, percentage;
    cout << "Enter marks for 5 subjects: ";
    for (int i = 0; i < 5; i++) {
        cin >> marks[i];
        total += marks[i];
    }

    percentage = (total / 500) * 100;

    cout << "Percentage: " << percentage << "%" << endl;
    if (percentage >= 60) {
        cout << "Grade: A" << endl;
    } else if (percentage >= 50) {
        cout << "Grade: B" << endl;
    } else if (percentage >= 40) {
        cout << "Grade: C" << endl;
    } else {
        cout << "Grade: Fail" << endl;
    }

    return 0;
}
21/05/2024, 09:46 - Saksham Singh Tomar Clg: 3rd number
21/05/2024, 09:46 - Saksham Singh Tomar Clg: #include <iostream>
using namespace std;

int main() {
    int num, reversedNum = 0, remainder;
    cout << "Enter an integer: ";
    cin >> num;

    while (num != 0) {
        remainder = num % 10;
        reversedNum = reversedNum * 10 + remainder;
        num /= 10;
    }

    cout << "Reversed Number: " << reversedNum << endl;

    return 0;
}

int main() {

27/11/2024, 11:22 - Saloni Clg CR: #include <iostream>
using namespace std;

// Function to swap two numbers using call by value
void swapByValue(int a, int b) {
    int temp = a;
    a = b;
    b = temp;
    cout << "Inside swapByValue - a: " << a << ", b: " << b << endl;
}

// Function to swap two numbers using call by reference
void swapByReference(int &a, int &b) {
    int temp = a;
    a = b;
    b = temp;
}

int main() {
    int num1, num2;

    // Input two numbers
    cout << "Enter the first number: ";
    cin >> num1;
    cout << "Enter the second number: ";
    cin >> num2;

    // Display original values
    cout << "\nBefore swapping:\n";
    cout << "num1: " << num1 << ", num2: " << num2 << endl;

    // Call swapByValue
    swapByValue(num1, num2);
    cout << "After swapByValue (original values unchanged):\n";
    cout << "num1: " << num1 << ", num2: " << num2 << endl;

    // Call swapByReference
    swapByReference(num1, num2);
    cout << "After swapByReference (original values swapped):\n";
    cout << "num1: " << num1 << ", num2: " << num2 << endl;

    return 0;
}

11/03/2025, 11:58 - Saloni Clg CR: *Institute of Technology and Management, Gwalior*

(*Nodal Centre*: Viksit Bharat Youth Parliament 2025 ‚Äì Gwalior District)

*NOTICE*
*Subject*: Participation in Viksit Bharat Youth Parliament 2025

All interested individuals aged *18-25 years* (as of 24th February 2025) from *Gwalior, Datia, Bhind, and Morena* districts are invited to participate in the Viksit Bharat Youth Parliament 2025. This event provides a platform for youth to express their ideas on national development and governance. 

*Eligibility*: Open to both students and non-students from the above-mentioned districts.

*Age limit*: 18-25 years as of 24th February 2025.

*Video Submission & Online Registration*

*Topic*: ‚ÄúWhat does Viksit Bharat mean to you?‚Äù
*Duration*: 1-minute video
*Language*: Hindi or English

*Registration & Video Upload Deadline*: 09 March 2025

*Registration Link*: https://mybharat.gov.in/pages/event_detail?event_name=Viksit-Bharat-Youth-Parliament-Nodal-District-Gwalior&key=978101396954

*Nodal-Level Youth parliament Competition 2025*

*Selection*: *150 participants* will be shortlisted from Gwalior, Datia, Bhind, and Morena.

*Mode:* Physical presentation at ITM Gwalior

*Topic*: "One Nation, One Election: Paving the Way for Viksit Bharat."

*Speech Duration*: 3 minutes
*Language*: Hindi or English

*Date & Time*: To be announced soon


*Selection for State-Level Competition*

After all 150 shortlisted participants present their speeches, 10 best candidates will be selected.

These 10 finalists will represent Nodal Gwalior at the State-Level Youth Parliament in physical mode.

*Venue*:
Institute of Technology and Management, Gwalior, Madhya Pradesh

For any queries, contact:
*Nodal Officer*: Prof. Narendra Kumar Verma
*Mobile No.*: 8109707108
*Email ID*: narendra.verma@itmgoi.in

This is your chance to be the voice of the nation! Participate and make a difference!

Thanks and regards

Prof. Narendra Kumar Verma
Nodal Officer, Viksit Bharat Youth Parliament 2025(Gwalior, Bhind, Morena and Datia)
Institute of Technology and Management, Gwalior

CREATE DATABASE company_db;

USE company_db;

-- 3. Create a table named 'employees'
CREATE TABLE employees (
    id INT PRIMARY KEY AUTO_INCREMENT,
    name VARCHAR(100),
    position VARCHAR(100),
    salary DECIMAL(10,2)
);

-- 4. Insert sample employee records
INSERT INTO employees (name, position, salary) VALUES
('Alice Johnson', 'Manager', 75000.00),
('Andrew Smith', 'Engineer', 70000.00),
('Brian Lee', 'Analyst', 60000.00),
('Amelia Davis', 'HR Executive', 65000.00),
('Charles Brown', 'Technician', 50000.00),
('Adam Cooper', 'Intern', 35000.00);

-- 5. Query: Find employees whose names start with 'A'
SELECT name
FROM employees
WHERE name LIKE 'A%';
